[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith a single test input in interactive fuzzing mode.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Issue Type  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The crash is classified by AddressSanitizer as a global-buffer-overflow [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mout-of-bounds write on global/static data[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Crash Location  [0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The overflow is detected at packet-gvcp.[0m[1;92mc:984[0m[39m in `dissect_register`. The [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbacktrace shows the path:  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. `dissect_register`  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. called by `dissect_writereg_cmd`  [0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. then `dissect_gvcp`  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. through the normal dissector invocation chain [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`call_dissector_…`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m  [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. and finally into the fuzzing entry point `LLVMFuzzerTestOneInput`.[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Memory Layout Observations  [0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  AddressSanitizer reports the bad write [0m[1;36m32[0m[39m bytes before `gvcp_register_value` [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39msize [0m[1;36m64[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and immediately after `gvcp_register_number` [0m[1;39m([0m[39msize [0m[1;36m64[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The shadow bytes [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mindicate a global redzone [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`f9`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m was violated, confirming an underflow relative to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe intended buffer region.[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Fuzzing Harness Context  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  The fuzzer is configured with `[0m[33mFUZZING_ENGINE[0m[39m=[0m[35mlibfuzzer[0m[39m` and [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[33mRUN_FUZZER_MODE[0m[39m=[0m[35minteractive[0m[39m`, invoking `[0m[35m/out/[0m[95mhandler_gvcp[0m[39m` with `-[0m[33mruns[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m100[0m[39m` on the[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprovided testcase. The harness disables unrelated protocol dissectors and focuses [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mon the GVCP dissector via `fuzzshark`. The harness itself only calls into the [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstandard Wireshark API [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`epan_dissect_run`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, so the root of the overflow resides in[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe GVCP dissector’s code.[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Affected Code Areas  [0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  Investigation should focus on the following source segments:  [0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • packet-gvcp.c around line [0m[1;36m984[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dissect_register`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and the data structures [0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • The command handlers in the same file [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`dissect_writereg_cmd`, overall [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`dissect_gvcp` logic[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that prepare and index into these global buffers.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    • Any helper routines or size checks that govern how many register entries are [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mparsed or written.[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Important Findings  [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The overflow is deterministic and reproducible with a single fuzzed input.  [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • The global buffers in question are statically sized but appear to be indexed or[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moffset incorrectly under certain input conditions.  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  • No other protocols or code paths are involved; this is isolated to the GVCP [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Overview and Root-Cause Analysis  [0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The global arrays `gvcp_register_number[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mGVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`gvcp_register_value[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mGVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT[0m[1;39m][0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39meach [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m entries[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are never [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds‐checked or reset per‐command.  [0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `dissect_writereg_cmd`, `num_registers = length/[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m` can exceed [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m, driving [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe loop [0m[1;39m([0m[39mand successive `dissect_register` calls[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m past the static array capacity. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Furthermore, `gvcp_register_count` is only zero‐initialized at program start, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mnot at the start of each WRITEREG command, so residual counts from previous [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcommands further exacerbate overflow.  [0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `dissect_register`, each call unconditionally writes to index [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`gvcp_register_count` and increments it, with no check against [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`GVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT`.  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Preservation of Existing Logic  [0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Valid WRITEREG packets that specify up to [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m register/value pairs will remain [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfully dissected and displayed, as before.  [0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The summary generation logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39miterating over the same global arrays to display[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mall writes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m is unchanged but is now guaranteed to stay within bounds.  [0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - No other dissectors, helper routines, or harness code are modified.  [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Patch Steps  [0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   A. Reset the Count at the Start of WRITEREG_CMD  [0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `packet-gvcp.c`, locate the top of `dissect_writereg_cmd` [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1774[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Immediately after computing `int num_registers = length [0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m;`, insert:[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Reset the global-write register buffers for this command *[0m[35m/[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     gvcp_register_count = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     This ensures each WRITEREG invocation starts with an empty buffer.  [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   B. Clamp the Number of Registers to the Static Limit  [0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Still in `dissect_writereg_cmd`, after resetting `gvcp_register_count`, add:[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnum_registers > GVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Too many register/value pairs in packet; truncate to avoid overflow *[0m[35m/[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       num_registers = GVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT;[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     Alternatively [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor additionally[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, you may emit an expert warning:[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_expert_format[0m[1;39m([0m[39mgvcp_telegram_tree, pinfo, [0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m&ei_gvcp_privileged_register,[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                  tvb, startoffset, [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m,[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                  [0m[32m"WRITEREG_CMD contains %d entries, truncating to [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m%d"[0m[39m,[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                  length/[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, GVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     This clamps the loop iteration to the array capacity and avoids any [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mout‐of‐bounds indexing.  [0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   C. Guard Array Writes in dissect_register  [0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - In `dissect_register` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnear line [0m[1;36m983[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, wrap the two global‐array writes with a[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbounds check:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mgvcp_register_count < GVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       gvcp_register_number[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mgvcp_register_count[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = addr;[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       gvcp_register_value[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mgvcp_register_count++[0m[1;39m][0m[39m = value;[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m[39m else [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       [0m[35m/[0m[39m* Extra entries beyond GVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT are dropped *[0m[35m/[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m       return [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[39m* or simply return, depending on expected return type *[0m[35m/[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     This secondary guard ensures that even if `dissect_register` is called out of [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthe normal WRITEREG_CMD loop [0m[1;39m([0m[39munlikely but defensive[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, no illegal writes occur.  [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   D. Verify Summary Logic  [0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The code that builds the summary tree:[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     for [0m[1;39m([0m[39muint32_t i = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m; i < gvcp_register_count; i++[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m … [0m[1;39m}[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     proto_item *summary = [0m[1;35mproto_tree_add_item[0m[1;39m([0m[39mtree, [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m, tvb, offset, [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mgvcp_register_count * [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m, ENC_NA[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     ```[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     now naturally iterates only over the clamped number of entries. No changes [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mneeded here.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Justification and Side-Effect Mitigation  [0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By resetting `gvcp_register_count` per WRITEREG command, we prevent stale [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mcounts from accumulating across multiple dissections.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - By clamping `num_registers` to `GVCP_MAX_REGISTER_COUNT`, we prevent a [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmalicious or malformed packet from specifying an excessive number of register/value[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpairs.  [0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - The bounds‐check in `dissect_register` serves as a last line of defense, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mensuring that even if upstream logic changes, out‐of‐bounds writes are impossible. [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Legitimate traffic with ≤[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m writes is unaffected; any packet with >[0m[1;36m16[0m[39m writes [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwill have only the first [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m processed, which is consistent with the static buffer [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdesign.  [0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - If desired, an expert notice can flag truncated commands to the user, but this[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mis optional.  [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Testing and Verification  [0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Rebuild Wireshark with AddressSanitizer enabled.  [0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Re-run the existing fuzz test that triggered the AddressSanitizer error. [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mConfirm no global-buffer-overflow is reported.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Manually craft a WRITEREG_CMD packet with, for instance, [0m[1;36m20[0m[39m register/value [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpairs; verify packets [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m–[0m[1;36m15[0m[39m are dissected, entries [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m+ are dropped or logged, and no[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmemory corruption occurs.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Run the complete test suite [0m[1;39m([0m[39mincluding all existing protocol dissector tests[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto ensure no regressions.  [0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis strategy fully addresses the overflow: it prevents count accumulation, [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39menforces the static array limit, and preserves existing dissection output for valid[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minputs without modifying harness or test code.  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
